                    <div id="legisContent">
                        <div class="legis"  id="legis"><div class="front"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="actHd"  id="aT-">Economic Expansion Incentives <br/>(Relief from Income Tax) <br/>Act 1967</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="revdHdr">2020 REVISED EDITION</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="revdTxt">This revised edition incorporates all amendments up to and including 1 December 2021 and comes into operation on 31 December 2021</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="longTitle"  id="al-">An Act relating to incentives for the establishment of pioneer industries and for economic expansion generally, by way of providing relief from income tax.</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="cDate">[15 December 1967]</td></tr></table></div><div class="body"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="part"  id="P11-"><div class="partNo">PART 1</div><table width="100%"><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P11-he-">PRELIMINARY</td></tr></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr1-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Short title</span></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>1.</strong>&#xA0;&#xA0;This Act is the Economic Expansion Incentives (Relief from Income Tax) Act 1967.</td></tr></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr2-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Act to be construed as one with Income Tax Act&#160;1947</span></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>2.</strong>&#xA0;&#xA0;This Act must, unless otherwise expressly provided for in this Act, be construed as one with the Income Tax Act&#160;1947.</td></tr></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr3-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Interpretation</span></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>3.</strong>&#xA0;&#xA0;In this Act, unless the context otherwise requires&#160;&#8212;<table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“approved activity”, in relation to a company, means an activity that has been approved under section 40A or 40E(1)(<em>b</em>) as an approved activity for the company;<div class="amendNote">[Act 39 of 2023 wef 01/04/2023]</div></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“approved activity certificate” means a certificate issued under section 40A(4)(<em>b</em>);<div class="amendNote">[Act 39 of 2023 wef 01/04/2023]</div></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“approved foreign loan” means a loan which is approved under section&#160;33 to be an approved foreign loan;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“approved royalties, fees or contributions” means royalties, technical assistance fees or contributions to research and development costs which have been approved under section&#160;37 to be approved royalties, fees or contributions;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“certificate” includes a letter or other document issued by the Minister to a company pursuant to an application made by the company under a provision of this Act;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“company” means any company incorporated or registered in accordance with the provisions of any written law relating to companies;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“Comptroller” means the Comptroller of Income Tax appointed under the Income Tax Act&#160;1947;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“foreign loan certificate” means a foreign loan certificate issued under section&#160;33;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“intellectual property income” means any intellectual property income prescribed by the Minister under section&#160;64;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“manufacture”, in relation to a product, includes any process or method used in making or developing the product;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“new trade or business” means the trade or business&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">in respect of any product or products specified in a single pioneer certificate of a pioneer enterprise; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">that is considered under section&#160;7 to have been set up and commenced on the day following the tax relief expiry date of the old trade or business in respect of that product or those products;</td></tr></table></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“old trade or business” means the trade or business of a pioneer enterprise which satisfies all of the following conditions:<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">it is in respect of one or more pioneer products specified in a single pioneer certificate of the pioneer enterprise;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">the part of the trade or business in respect of each pioneer product is carried on during the tax relief period for that product;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">it either ceases before or is considered, under section&#160;7, to have permanently ceased on the tax relief expiry date;</td></tr></table></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“pioneer certificate” means a pioneer certificate issued under section&#160;5;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“pioneer enterprise” means any company which has been approved by the Minister under section&#160;5 for a pioneer product and to which a pioneer certificate is issued under that section;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“pioneer industry” means an industry approved under section&#160;4 to be a pioneer industry;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“pioneer product” means a product approved under section&#160;4 to be a pioneer product;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“production day”, in relation to a pioneer product that is approved under section&#160;5(3) for a pioneer enterprise, means the date specified in the pioneer enterprise’s pioneer certificate under section&#160;5(5)(<em>b</em>) or (7)(<em>a</em>) or (<i>c</i>) as the production day of that product;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“productive equipment” means machinery or plant which would normally qualify for deduction under sections&#160;19, 19A, 20, 21 and 22 of the Income Tax Act&#160;1947;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“royalties, fees or contributions certificate” means a certificate issued under section&#160;37;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“royalties or technical assistance fees” includes&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">any royalties, rentals or other amounts paid as consideration for the use of, or the right to use, copyright, scientific works, patents, designs, plans, secret processes, formulae, trade marks, licences or other like property or rights;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">income derived from the alienation of property or information mentioned in paragraph&#160;(<em>a</em>); and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">other amounts paid in consideration of services rendered by a non-resident person or the person’s employee in connection with the use of property or rights belonging to, or the initial operation of any plant, machinery or other apparatus purchased from, the non-resident person,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="defSO"  style="font-size:13pt">but does not include royalties, rentals or other amounts paid in respect of the operation of mines, quarries or other places of extraction of natural resources; or fees paid to an individual for the performance of professional services in Singapore other than as an employee;</td></tr></table></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“tax” means income tax imposed by the Income Tax Act&#160;1947;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“tax relief expiry date”, in relation to an old trade or business, means&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">where the old trade or business is in respect of only one pioneer product, the date on which the tax relief period for that pioneer product expires; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">where the old trade or business is in respect of 2 or more pioneer products, the date on which all the tax relief periods for those products expire, or (if the Minister has removed one or more but not all of those products from the pioneer certificate under section 5, or extended the tax relief period or periods for one or more but not all of those products under section 6) the date of expiry of the tax relief period with the latest date of expiry.<div class="amendNote">[1/2012; 11/2016; 8/2018]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr3A-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Assignment of function or power to public body </span></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>3A.</strong><a name="pr3A-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">&#8212;(1)&#xA0;&#xA0;This section applies where the Minister, by notification in the <em>Gazette</em>, assigns a function or power under a provision of this Act (called in this section an incentive provision) to —<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a public body for which the Minister is the responsible Minister; or </td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a public body for which the Minister is not the responsible Minister, after consultation with the responsible Minister of the public body.</td></tr></table></span><a name="pr3A-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&#xA0;&#xA0;Starting on the date the Minister assigns a function or power under an incentive provision to a public body in accordance with subsection (1), a reference to the Minister in that incentive provision includes a reference to the public body. </td></tr></table><a name="pr3A-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&#xA0;&#xA0;An assignment by the Minister is subject to such limitations as the Minister may impose.</td></tr></table><a name="pr3A-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&#xA0;&#xA0;The public body, when carrying out a function or exercising a power under an incentive provision, is treated as carrying out a function or exercising a power conferred on the public body under the Act that establishes it. </td></tr></table><a name="pr3A-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&#xA0;&#xA0;The public body must carry out a function or exercise a power under an incentive provision in accordance with any directions given by the Minister.</td></tr></table><a name="pr3A-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&#xA0;&#xA0;A member of the public body who is not from the public sector must not be involved in the carrying out of a function or the exercise of a power under an incentive provision by the public body.</td></tr></table><a name="pr3A-ps7-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(7)&#xA0;&#xA0;The public body must not delegate a function or power under an incentive provision to any of its members, or to any other person, who is not from the public sector.</td></tr></table><a name="pr3A-ps8-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(8)&#xA0;&#xA0;Without affecting any obligation as to secrecy or other restriction against the disclosure of information imposed by any law or contract —<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a member of the public body who is from the public sector; or </td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a person to whom a function or power under an incentive provision has been delegated, </td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">that receives or obtains information relating to a person for the purposes of an incentive provision, must not disclose or provide access to such information to a member of the public body, or any other person, who is not from the public sector. </td></tr></table></td></tr></table><a name="pr3A-ps9-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(9)&#xA0;&#xA0;Subsection (8) does not apply to the following information:<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">information the disclosure of which has been approved by the Minister; </td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">information relating to a person —<table class="p2_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr id="pr3A-ps9-p1b-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">for which consent for disclosure has been obtained from the person; or </td></tr><tr id="pr3A-ps9-p1b-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">that is already in the possession of the public body; </td></tr></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">information that is publicly available.</td></tr></table></td></tr></table><a name="pr3A-ps10-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(10)&#xA0;&#xA0;The public body may carry out a function or exercise a power under an incentive provision despite the absence of a quorum at any meeting of the public body because of subsection (6) or (8), and the absence of a quorum does not affect the validity of anything done by the public body at the meeting. </td></tr></table><a name="pr3A-ps11-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(11)&#xA0;&#xA0;An assignment of a function or power under an incentive provision in accordance with subsection (1) does not affect or prevent the carrying out of any function or exercise of any power by the Minister. </td></tr></table><a name="pr3A-ps12-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(12)&#xA0;&#xA0;This section does not permit the assignment of —<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any power to make subsidiary legislation; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the power in section 60(2).</td></tr></table></td></tr></table><a name="pr3A-ps13-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(13)&#xA0;&#xA0;To avoid doubt, this section applies in addition to, and not in derogation of, section 36 of the Interpretation Act 1965.</td></tr></table><a name="pr3A-ps14-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(14)&#xA0;&#xA0;In this section —<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a person is from the public sector if the person is a public officer or an employee of a public body; and </td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">“public body” and “responsible Minister”, in relation to a public body, have the meanings given by section 2(1) of the Public Sector (Governance) Act 2018.<div class="amendNote">[Act 9 of 2022 wef 22/04/2022]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></div></td></tr></table><div class="dms" data-field="seriesId" data-term="5a31858f-939a-4817-8d42-99cd443548e2"></div><div
